msg:We, an old couple, came to Kunming with our two children to escape the summer heat. We first chose the Sunac Shibago Hotel in the Sunac Cultural and Tourism City. We especially chose the parent-child suite. When we arrived at the hotel, we were first warmly received by the front desk staff Xiaobu and Li Ting. , and gave us professional travel guidance, making us feel at home. When we arrived at the hotel, it was not check-in time yet. They were always considerate of the guests and checked in for us in advance, which made us feel extremely warm. The guest rooms are warm and cute, and the bedding is high-end and comfortable. Especially the children's room is specially equipped with a children's slide, a children's toilet, a complete range of children's toiletries, and children's dolls that children can't put down. Originally booked for 1 night, but later extended the stay for 3 more nights. During the stay, the baby was accidentally bitten by a bee on the balcony. Manager Wang at the front desk found some medicines such as Fengyoujing and iodine for the child. Hearing that white vinegar can relieve the redness and swelling of bee bites, Manager Wang ran to the kitchen and found White vinegar, thank you so much. I will definitely stay here again next summer to escape the heat.
